### African liberation events
###
### Participants:
### ANG - Angola
### GUI - Guinea
### LIB - Liberia 
### MOR - Morroco
### MOZ - Mozambique
### U03 - Beninkongo
### SAF - South Africa
### U29 - Algerie
### U04 - Sahel
### U05 - Bantu Federation

##### Conférence Africaine de l'Internationale

		exists = U04
		exists = VIC
                war = { country = U04 country = VIC }
                war = { country = U29 country = VIC }
		event = 777114
		NOT = { 
		alliance = { country = U04 country = U29 }
		}
		}

	name = "Alliance with Guinea?"
	desc = "Just like us, the Guineans are also undertaking a liberation struggle against National France. According to the dictates of the Conférence, all African independence movements should join forces!"

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1939 }
	offset = 10
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1966 }

	action_a = {
	name = "Invite them into an alliance"
	ai_chance = 95
 		command = { type = trigger which = 777394 }
                command = { type = dissent value = -5 }
                command = { type = belligerence which = U29 value = 5  }
                command = { type = relation which = U04 value = 50 }
	}
	action_b = {
	name = "We are better alone, actually"
	ai_chance = 5
		command = { type = dissent value = 1 }
                command = { type = belligerence which = U29 value = -2  }
                command = { type = relation which = U29 value = -20 }
	}
}

 		command = { type = alliance which = U29 }
                command = { type = dissent value = -5 }
                command = { type = belligerence which = U04 value = 5  }
                command = { type = relation which = U29 value = 50 }
	}
	action_b = {
	name = "We are better alone, actually"
	ai_chance = 0
		command = { type = dissent value = 1 }
                command = { type = belligerence which = U04 value = -2  }

	}

event = {
	id = 777128
	random = no
	country = FRA
	style = 2
	picture = "westafrica"

	trigger = { 
		control = { province = 966 data = FRA }	# FRA holds Conakry
		NOT = {
		exists = GUI
		exists = VIC
		}
		}

	name = "The Commune of Guinea"
	desc = "With National France defeated and great parts of their former territory in our hands, we now have the opportunity to declare the independence of a friendly Republic of Guinea!"

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1939 }
	offset = 100
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1966 }

	action_a = {
	name = "Grant them their independence"
	ai_chance = 95
		command = { type = independence which = GUI value = 1 }
		command = { type = trigger which = 777129 }
		command = { type = sleepevent which = 777130 }
	}
	action_b = {
	name = "We'd rather keep rulling the area directly"
	ai_chance = 5
		command = { type = dissent value = 2 }
	}
}

        name = "Our offer was refused!"
        command = { type = dissent value = 3 }
    }

    action_b = {
        ai_chance = 50
        name = "Our offer was accepted!"
        command = { type = dissent value = -4 }
        command = { type = supplies value = -2000 }
        command = { type = money value = -500  }
        command = { type = domestic which = freedom value = 1 }
        command = { type = domestic which = political_left value = 1  }
        command = { type = sleepevent which = 777204 }
        command = { type = independence which = ANG value = 1 when = 0 }
        command = { type = make_puppet which = ANG }
    }

### SAF and Mittelafrika

### First alliance proposal

event = {
	id = 777257
	random = no
	country = SAF
	style = 2
	picture = "Rapallo_conference"

	trigger = { 
		flag = AFR_CONFERENCE_2
		event = 777055
                exists = CON
		OR = {
		war = { country = CON country = ANG }
		war = { country = CON country = MOZ }
		war = { country = CON country = U05 }
		war = { country = CON country = U03 }
		war = { country = VIC country = U04 }
		war = { country = VIC country = U29 }
		war = { country = VIC country = GUI }
		} 
		NOT = {
                government = { type = communist country = CON }
		government = communist
		alliance = { country = CON country = SAF }
		alliance = { country = CON country = GER }
		alliance = { country = SAF country = GER }
		alliance = { country = SAF country = CAN }
		alliance = { country = SAF country = VIC }
                alliance = { country = SAF country = FRA }
		war = { country = SAF country = CON }
		ispuppet = CON
		ispuppet = SAF
		}
		}

	name = "Syndicalism threatening South Africa and Mittelafrika"
	desc = "With the German Empire defeated in Europe, the Internationale has decided to bring their ideology of hate to the African continent. Not only South Africa, but both National France and Mittelafrika already had to deal with socialist uprisings over the past months. Due to this, some in our foreign services believe in crafting an alliance with our northern neighbours in Mittelafrika for our mutual protection."

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1939 }
	offset = 50
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1966 }

	action_a = {
	ai_chance = 50
	name = "Our security depends on that - Propose an alliance to Mittelafrika"
		command = { type = trigger which = 777258 }
                command = { type = dissent value = -5 }
                command = { type = belligerence which = SAF value = 2  }
                command = { type = relation which = CON value = 50 }
	}
	action_b = {
	ai_chance = 50
	name = "We don't need anything from Mittelafrika"
		command = { type = dissent value = 1 }
                command = { type = relation which = CON value = -10 }
	}
}

event = {
	id = 777258
	random = no
	country = CON
	style = 2
	picture = "Rapallo_conference"

	name = "Alliance proposal from South Africa"
	desc = "After a Syndicalist uprising by the African National Congress nearly toppled the government of South Africa, Johannesburg has sent us a proposal for an alliance in order to fight the red menace in our continent. Should we accept their proposal?"

	action_a = {
	ai_chance = 70
	name = "Accept - Form the Johannesburg - Dar-es-Salaam axis"
		command = { type = alliance which = SAF }
                command = { type = dissent value = -5 }
                command = { type = belligerence which = CON value = 2  }
                command = { type = relation which = SAF value = 50 }
	}
	action_b = {
	ai_chance = 30
	name = "Refuse - We don't need anything from South Africa"
		command = { type = dissent value = 1 }
                command = { type = relation which = SAF value = -20 }
	}
}

### Unalligned SAF seizes Namibia

event = {
	id = 777259
	random = no
	country = SAF
	style = 2
	picture = "namibia"

	trigger = { 
		flag = AFR_CONFERENCE_2
                owned = { province = 884 data = CON }
                control = { province = 884 data = CON } 
		OR = {
		war = { country = CON country = ANG }
		war = { country = CON country = MOZ }
		war = { country = CON country = U05 }
                war = { country = CON country = U03 }
		} 
		NOT = {
		alliance = { country = CON country = SAF }
		alliance = { country = CON country = GER }
		alliance = { country = SAF country = GER }
		alliance = { country = SAF country = CAN }
		alliance = { country = SAF country = VIC }
		war = { country = SAF country = CON }
		ispuppet = SAF
		ispuppet = CON
                exists = NAM
		}
		}

	name = "Mittelafrika in chaos"
	desc = "The Freistaat Mittealfrika is facing major Syndicalist rebellions, which could very well result in South Africa being left with hostile left-wing powers right on her borders. But this crisis could also serve as an opportunity for us to expand our borders. We could minimize the threat by ordering our army to occupy the Mittelafrikan distrikt of Sudwestafrika (also known as Namibia), before the rebels have this same idea..."

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1939 }
	offset = 20
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1966 }

	action_a = {
	ai_chance = 80
	name = "Seize the opportunity and occupy Namibia"
		command = { type = trigger which = 777260 }
                command = { type = sleepevent which = 777264 }
                command = { type = relation which = CON value = -50 }
                command = { type = belligerence which = SAF value = 3  }
                command = { type = addcore   which = 885   }
                command = { type = addcore   which = 886   }
                command = { type = addcore   which = 882   }
                command = { type = addcore   which = 883   }
                command = { type = addcore   which = 884   }
	}
	action_b = {
	ai_chance = 20
	name = "We shouldn't annoy the Mittelafrikans"
		command = { type = dissent value = 1 }
                command = { type = relation which = CON value = 50 }
                command = { type = belligerence which = SAF value = -3  }
	}
}

##### Borderfixing! Euro powers releasing provinces to the Africans

##### Beninkongo

event = {
	id = 777297
	random = no
	country = U03
	style = 2
	picture = "diplomatic_campaign"

	trigger = { 
		government = communist
		NOT = {
                atwar = U03
		exists = VIC
		exists = CON
		}
		}

	name = "Relations with the Internationale"
	desc = "With the war against Mittelafrika over, we are ready to fully establish diplomatic relations with the Internationale powers."

	date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1939 }
	offset = 150
	deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1966 }
